** Please check uvw_FW_USER when upgrade engine to make sure users that belong to deleted distributor not able to login.
** In order to view the map, please open "Default.aspx" in any text editor, then put a script tag in side of <head> tag.
** Script to put : <script type="text/javascript" src="http://maps.googleapis.com/maps/api/js?sensor=false"></script>

0033241: Inventory > Stock Adjustment > found 'Allocated Quantity' and 'Adjustable Quantity' is not auto-populated based expiry date.
Remarks:
    Root Cause: - No checking with the key-in quantity with the adjustable quantity.
    Solution: - Applied the quantity checking and pop up a message if value was invalid.
    Page Changed: - pag_I_StkAdj_NewGeneral_ExpDt

0033328: Transaction > Invoice > found txn_invpromo removed if direct re-apply promotion without any editing for picked Order
Remarks:
(1) Transaction > Order > Promotion > Apply: Promotion budget exceed message prompt even balance still less than promo discount.
    Root Cause: - It compare the discount value with the (Balance - Soft Allocate).
    Solution: - Compare only the Balance whether less than discount value.
    Page Changed - Promotion

(2) Transaction > Order > Promotion > Apply: Discount Amount is displayed from the listing.
    Root Cause: - Both values of Discount fields does not been cleared when promotion is over budget.
    Solution: - Clear the values and recalculate the discount.
    Page Changed - Promotion

(3) Transaction > Order > Process Order: Promotion Block windows pop-up.
    Root Cause: - It take the balance as "BALANCE - SOFT_ALLOC - HARD_ALLOC" to check whether it is less than Discount Amount.
    Solution: - Changed to take the balance as "BALANCE" amount to check the Promotion Block.
    DB Changed: - SBE_PROCESS_ORDER

(4) Transaction > Invoice > Deallocate: BALANCE and SOFT_ALLOC has been updated even CLAIMABLE_IND = 0.
    Root Cause: - No condition with the checking CLAIMABLE_IND = 1.
    Solution: - Update the BALANCE and SOFT_ALLOC when CLAIMABLE_IND = 1.
    DB Changed: - SBE_DEALLOCATE_INVOICE
